  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;

    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;

  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);

  }

    display: block;

  }

  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically

  .medium-heading {

        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;

        }

          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        <p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





An extension with access to the "chrome.debugger" API can attach to tabs



<span class="line"><!---->An extension with access to the "chrome.debugger" API can attach to tabs<!----></span>



<br>





displaying a security interstitial without requiring higher privileges as



<span class="line"><!---->displaying a security interstitial without requiring higher privileges as<!----></span>



<br>





such dialogs are loaded in a regular web renderer process outside the



<span class="line"><!---->such dialogs are loaded in a regular web renderer process outside the<!----></span>



<br>





"chrome://" scheme (kUnreachableWebDataURL).



<span class="line"><!---->"chrome://" scheme (kUnreachableWebDataURL).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





An attacker who convinced a user to install a malicious extension can then



<span class="line"><!---->An attacker who convinced a user to install a malicious extension can then<!----></span>



<br>





evaluate a JavaScript expression to modify the security message or skip it



<span class="line"><!---->evaluate a JavaScript expression to modify the security message or skip it<!----></span>



<br>





altogether when a proceed button is available.



<span class="line"><!---->altogether when a proceed button is available.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 95.0.4638.69 stable



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 95.0.4638.69 stable<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 10 21H1, OS build 19043.1320



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 10 21H1, OS build 19043.1320<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. Install and enable the provided extension



<span class="line"><!---->1. Install and enable the provided extension<!----></span>



<br>





2. Trigger an interstitial (e.g., by visiting 



<span class="line"><!---->2. Trigger an interstitial (e.g., by visiting <!----></span>





https://expired.badssl.com/



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://expired.badssl.com/"><!---->https://expired.badssl.com/<!----></a>



<br>





   or 



<span class="line"><!---->   or <!----></span>





https://testsafebrowsing.appspot.com/s/phishing.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://testsafebrowsing.appspot.com/s/phishing.html"><!---->https://testsafebrowsing.appspot.com/s/phishing.html<!----></a>





)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The PoC extension will automatically skip the interstitial without



<span class="line"><!---->The PoC extension will automatically skip the interstitial without<!----></span>



<br>





requiring further user interaction.



<span class="line"><!---->requiring further user interaction.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CREDIT INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->CREDIT INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Reporter credit: José Miguel Moreno



<span class="line"><!---->Reporter credit: José Miguel Moreno<!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->Computer Security Lab (COSEC) at UC3M<!----></span>

Interesting find!



<span class="line"><!---->Interesting find!<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This is explicitly allowed here [1], which was added here [2] as part of 



<span class="line"><!---->This is explicitly allowed here [1], which was added here [2] as part of <!----></span>





issue 882589



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=882589" title="(extension) inspector unexpectedly detaches when offline and reloading"><!---->issue 882589<!----></a>





.  The intention there was to allow the extension to stay connected if the web page threw an error (with "offline" as the main error motivating the change) - that's, I think, still desirable.  But we probably don't want to allow extensions to modify interstitials.



<span class="line"><!---->.  The intention there was to allow the extension to stay connected if the web page threw an error (with "offline" as the main error motivating the change) - that's, I think, still desirable.  But we probably don't want to allow extensions to modify interstitials.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





nasko@, lukasza@ - would it make sense to serve security interstitials at a different address than other errors?  Alternatively, we might be able to look at the WebContennts' last commit error code and make a determination there - but it'd be simpler if we could just filter on URL.



<span class="line"><!---->nasko@, lukasza@ - would it make sense to serve security interstitials at a different address than other errors?  Alternatively, we might be able to look at the WebContennts' last commit error code and make a determination there - but it'd be simpler if we could just filter on URL.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tentatively passing this to danilsomsikov as a debugger owner.



<span class="line"><!---->Tentatively passing this to danilsomsikov as a debugger owner.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

To answer your question in C#17, CVE IDs are assigned at the time a the fix for the issue ships in a stable channel release. As this is a low severity issue, the fix has not yet shipped in a stable channel release. It appears it was landed in 103 and will ship with the 103 stable channel release Tuesday, June 24 and will receive a CVE at that time.
